</p>

<p><b>бле́д<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b> (<span title="написание в дореформенной орфографии" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">дореформ.</span> <span style="font-family: | Palatino Linotype | ">блѣдный</span>)
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a/c'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>бледне́е, <a href = vnd.unilang:бледнеть.html>бледне́й</a>.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-бледн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blěskъ</i>

***блеснуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ть</a> (5356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blьsknǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blesnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shine, to glitter, to sparkle, to flash</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be gifted with, to shine with, to sparkle with (+ instrumental)</li>
<li>to flash across one's mind <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá <b>blesnúla</b> myslʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the thought flashed across my mind</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***блестеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a> (2515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blestétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shine, to glitter, to sparkle, to flash</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be gifted with, to shine with, to sparkle with (+ instrumental)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>бле́щет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>умо́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>bléščet</b> umóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is not gifted with intelligence, he is not a genius</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means the same thing as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blestétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> but the latter is also used figuratively. Present tense forms can coincide.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***блеф.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блеф.html>блеф</a> (24120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Since the 1920s from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bluff</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:близиться.html>бли́зиться</a> (13305)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близ.html>близ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bliz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близиться.html>бли́зиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blízitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to draw near, to approach
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:близиться.html>бли́зиться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>концу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blízitʹsja</b> k koncú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">draw/come to a close</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blizъkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близкий.html>бли́зкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blízkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бли́же</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ближайший.html>ближа́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>close, near</li>
<li>dear, intimate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>directly concerning <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>having free access <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>similar <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:близлежащий.html>близлежа́щий</a> (15239)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1766. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близ.html>близ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bliz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́щий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ležáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nahegelegen</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nächstliegend</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близлежащий.html>близлежа́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blizležáščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>nearby, close by</li>
<li>contiguous, adjacent, neighboring</li></ol>

***близнец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близне́ц</a> (6786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bliznьcь</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">близна́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bliznák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">bliźniak</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">blizanac</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близне́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bliznéc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близнеца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близнецы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близнец.html>близнецо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>twin</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:близорукий.html>близору́кий</a> (13224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">близозоръкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blizozorŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with haplology.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близорукий.html>близору́кий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blizorúkij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>nearsighted, myopic</li>
<li>shortsighted, lacking in foresight</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блинчик.html>бли́нчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blínčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блинчик.html>бли́нчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блинчик.html>бли́нчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блинчик.html>бли́нчиков</a></b>)

***блистать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a> (8705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blistátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеснуть.html>блесну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shine, to glitter, to sparkle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a brilliant display, to shine, to be radiant (with), to be conspicuous (by)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красото́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молодость.html>мо́лодостью</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blistátʹ</b> krasotój i mólodostʹju</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to shine (be radiant) with youth and beauty</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блистать.html>блиста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blistátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means the same thing as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blestétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> but is also used figuratively. Present tense forms can coincide.</li></ul>

***блокада.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a> (5760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Blockade</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blokáda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> siege, blockade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a></b> ленингра́да <a href = vnd.unilang:длиться.html>дли́лась</a> 900 <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дней</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blokáda</b> Leningráda dlílasʹ 900 dnej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the siege of Leningrad lasted 900 days</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blockade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономический.html>экономи́ческая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ekonomíčeskaja <b>blokáda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">economic blockade</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> block; blocking; obstruction</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">siege</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осада.html>оса́да</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osáda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оцепление.html>оцепле́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oceplénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружение.html>окруже́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">okružénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>штурм</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šturm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокада.html>блока́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blokáda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокадный.html>блока́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blokádnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> under siege, blockade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блокадный.html>блока́дный</a></b> ленингра́д</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blokádnyj</b> Leningrád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Leningrad under siege</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blockade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> block; blocking; obstruction</li></ol>
